6.3. 
IZIMPENDULO EZILINDELEKILE ZEMIBUZO 
EMIFUSHANE 

1.1. 
Yindlela azishaya ngayo isifuba ezikhukhumeza ngomsebenzi 
wakhe wokusiza abantu nokwaziwa kwakhe abelungu abakhulu 
kanye nokwehla enyuka nezincwadi ezimbongayo nesheke lomuntu 
ahamba ezikhangisa ngalo kubantu. (3) 

1.2. 
Iziwula yilifa lezihlakaniphi: Lesi simo sokukhuluma siyayigqamisa 
inhloso kaNdebenkulu nomsebenzi athi uwuzele lapha 
eNyanyadu ngoba vele uzele khona ukuzogebenga aluthe abantu 
basemaphandleni ababona beyiziphukuphuku, beyilifa lakhe. Into 
ayizele lapha eNyanyadu akukhona ukuzosiza abantu basemakhaya, 
kodwa ufikele kona ukuzotapa umcebo wezinkomo zabo kubona 
ngoba yena ethi uhlakaniphile nakhu phela uvela edolobheni. (4) 
1.3. 
Yebo inguye uSathane ngoba nonezindodla zayo akadeli. Uyise 
uMkhwanazi ucebile unemfuyo kodwa usezoze alahlekelwe yimfuyo 
yakhe ngoba esazibona empofu esafuna okungaphezu kwalokho 
anakho. (2) 
1.4. 
Wayesebenza khona ukukhohlisa nokugebenga abantu ngisho 
nabafelokazi imbala ukuze aziphilise. (3) 
1.5 
Ukuvezwa komlingiswa onguThemba esiqeshini esicashuniwe: 
Okokuqala nje umbhali umnike leli gama likaThemba ngoba 
uyilo ngempela ithemba lalapha kwaMkhwanazi. Sekuthunywa 
yena, ubalandela iposi, naleli phepha alifundayo eliqukethe 
isixwayiso esibalulekile maqondana nobugebengu osebudlangile 
obunjengalobu abusolayo lapha kuNdebenkulu, libuye naye. Lesi 
sexwayiso ngokubona kwabo benodadewabo uThoko, sizigcwalisa 
ngokusobala izinsolo abanazo ngobugebengu ababubonayo kulo 
Ndebenkulu uMkhwanazi angasafuni kuzwa lutho ngaye. 
Isu alisebenzisile umbhali kulesi siqeshana, yilelo lokusebenzisa 

inkulumo mpendulwano ukubenza baphile abalingiswa bakhe. 
Sithola uThemba noThoko lapha bephawula ngokwenzekile 
nangokwenzekayo lapha ekhaya ngenxa yokufika kukaNdebenkulu 
onunusela abazali babo ngezizumbulu zemali athi bangayithola 
uma yena ebathengisela izinkomo zabo kubelungu bezindali 
nabamasilaha. 


UThemba simthola lapha ebuveza ngokusobala ubuhlungu 
abuzwayo enhliziyweni yakhe ngale nto eyenzekayo kuyise 
yokuluthwa uNdebenkulu. Umqondo wakhe umtshela ngokusobala 
ukuthi lo muntu onguNdebenkulu akaqondile, kanti phela 
wamuzwa kahle futhi uNdebenkulu ekhuluma noyise ethi iziwula 
yilifa lezihlakaniphi, okusho ukuthi isiwula nguye uMkhwanazi yena 
uyisihlakaniphi esizokudla izinkomo zikaMkhwanazi. 

UThemba simthola lapha ebuveza ngokusobala ubuhlungu 
abuzwayo enhliziyweni yakhe ngale nto eyenzekayo kuyise 
yokuluthwa uNdebenkulu. Umqondo wakhe umtshela ngokusobala 
ukuthi lo muntu onguNdebenkulu akaqondile, kanti phela 
wamuzwa kahle futhi uNdebenkulu ekhuluma noyise ethi iziwula 
yilifa lezihlakaniphi, okusho ukuthi isiwula nguye uMkhwanazi yena 
uyisihlakaniphi esizokudla izinkomo zikaMkhwanazi. 

1.6. 
Uthanda kakhulu imali nakhu useke waliphatha ngezandla isheke 
elifike noNdebenkulu ukuze abakhohlise bakhohliseke ngempela 
bayikholwe nento ayishoyo uma ethi imali iyatholakala ngokudayisa 
izinkomo. Izincwadi ezimbongayo nazo zimenza uMkhwanazi 
amkholwe ngempela uNdebenkulu. (3) 
1.7. 
Esinye sezifundo ezitholakalayo kule noveli yilesi sokuqaphelisa 
abantu ukuthi bangabohamba bethemba bonke abantu abangabazi 
ngoba bebathembisa ukubasiza futhi bebukeka bethembekile 
ngoba bayozithola sebelahlekelwa okukhona ngokungekho. (2) 
1.8. 
Ohlaba eyakhe akalelwa kusho ukuthi ngeke umvimbe umuntu ngoba 
yilowo nalowo uzenzela akuthandayo ngalokho okungokwakhe. (2) 

1.9. 
Ekugcineni uNdebenkulu esethi usephumelele ukubawaka izinkomo 
oShandu, kanti akabuzanga elangeni, izinto zizomjikela ngomzuzu 
wokugcina aboshwe zisale phansi izinkomo lezo esedalulekile 
ukuthi kanti uyisigebengu ebesivele sifunwa ngamaphoyisa. (3) 
IZIMPENDULO ZOMBUZO OMUDE 

a) 
UMkhwanazi 

Lona ngumlingiswa omkhulu kule noveli. Indaba yonke ingaye. 
Ugqamile. Konke okwenzekayo kule noveli, kuncike kuye. Umbhali 
umveze njengomuntu ongaswele lutho, omi kahle, onempahla egcwele 
isibaya, kodwa ngenxa yokununuselwa wuNdebenkulu ngemali, 
usezibona empofu esefuna okungaphezulu kwalokhu anakho. Umveze 
njengomlingiswa oguqukayo futhi wazibeka nezizathu zokuguquka 
kwakhe. Bekuhleziwe ngokuthula kwaMkhwanazi, kepha ngokufika 
kukaNdebenkulu zashintsha izinto. UMkhwanazi useke asikaze 
nokubashaya nakhu phela useyindlondlo nje eseyifuna ukujabulisa 
isivakashi sakwakhe esesicishe sadla isibaya sakhe sonke ngenxa 
yobudedengu bukaThemba nonina uMaNtuli. 
Usebona nokuthi uThemba noMaNtuli banamakhanda aluhlaza 
angaphekiwe. Usebone neqiniso alivezelwe wuNdebenkulu naye 
athi kade ayelisola lokuthi abafazi basemaphandleni banemiqondo 
ebuthuntu, ephenduka kancane okwesondo lenqola. Usebona nokuthi 
umkakhe unethuku, usesangene ngoba nakhu embuza ukuthi uzoze 
ahlabise uNdebenkulu imvu nje umazelaphi ngoba zolo lokhu kade 
kufike umntakadadewabo kaMaNtuli wenqaba ukumhlabisa ngoba ethi 
izimvu ziqedwe wukufa. Usembiza nangento engafundanga eyagcina 
ebangeni le-4 kanti kwasayena uMkhwanazi wagcina kulelo banga. 
UMkhwanazi usezibona engcono kakhulu njengoba enesivakashi 
esiyisikhulu esazana nabelungu abakhulu. 
Njengoba nasemhlanganweni owawubizwe uNdebenkulu nguye 


owayenguMgcinisihlalo nje wayesezibona naye eseyisikhulu, 
engumakhonya, engawuvala yena umhlangano uma abantu 
bengamlaleli. Simbona ethathekile impela yindaba kaNdebenkulu 
nezinkomo ezizomlethela imali eningi kangangoba lo moya usewufake 
nakuMaNtuli obekade engayiboni kahle le ndaba kaNdebenkulu. 
Ekugcineni sekuvelile ukuthi yisigebengu lesi asecishe wasihambisa 
nezinkomo zakhe, simbona ephelelwa amandla nenhliziyo yakhe 
isishaya ngamandla, eselibona iphutha alenzileyo lapho esethi ?Kazi 
uMaNtuli uyothini?? 

owayenguMgcinisihlalo nje wayesezibona naye eseyisikhulu, 
engumakhonya, engawuvala yena umhlangano uma abantu 
bengamlaleli. Simbona ethathekile impela yindaba kaNdebenkulu 
nezinkomo ezizomlethela imali eningi kangangoba lo moya usewufake 
nakuMaNtuli obekade engayiboni kahle le ndaba kaNdebenkulu. 
Ekugcineni sekuvelile ukuthi yisigebengu lesi asecishe wasihambisa 
nezinkomo zakhe, simbona ephelelwa amandla nenhliziyo yakhe 
isishaya ngamandla, eselibona iphutha alenzileyo lapho esethi ?Kazi 
uMaNtuli uyothini?? 

Ungumlingiswa obalulekile. Konke ukwenza nokuziphatha komlingiswa 
omkhulu, uMkhwanazi kuncike kuye. Ukufika kwakhe kwaMkhwanazi 
kuletha uthuthuva ngenxa yokuthi uMkhwanazi ufuna ukumjabulisa. 
Uze amhlabise imvu. 
UNdebenkulu uvezwe njengomlingiswa onehaba, umbhali agqamisa 
ukuziphatha kwakhe ngokumenza inhlekisa. Indlela azikhukhumeza 
ngayo najivaza ngayo abantu basemakhaya imenza abe yinto ehlekisayo. 
Umenza aphile impilo engelona iqiniso, engakholeki ukuze akhohlise 
laba bantu basemaphandleni ukuze abagebenge kahle. Nakhu phela 
uze asho nokuthi iziwula ziyifa lezihlakaniphi. 
Uvezwe futhi njengomuntu othanda ukubukwa. Nasesontweni uyilokhu 
ebheka emuva eqalaza abantu ukuthi bayambona yini njengoba 
ephakathi kwabo bengabasemaphandleni yena engumuntu omkhulu 
ohlala edolobheni. Uhluleka nawukuzehlisa eyilokhu eshaya isikhwehlela 
esincane esontweni, esulana nezibuko azifakile kodwa ebe engaculi 
nakuba iculo eliphethe elivulile. 
Umveze njengomkhohlisi, usemqedile uMkhwanazi emtshela ngezimali 
ezitholakala ngokudayisa izinkomo eze efakazisa nangesheke aliphethe. 
Pho, uMkhwanazi wayeke walithintaphi isheke lemali engaka! 


Ekugcineni izinkomo zoMkhwanazi noShandu sezisesiteshini, 
esezohamba nazo ngempela umfo kaNdebenkulu, sekuyadaluleka 
ukuthi kanti uyisigebengu esikade sifunwa amaphoyisa esasizibize ngoEE 
Mlomo eMnambithi ngenkathi siqola umfelokazi izinkomo ayezishiyelwe 
umyeni wakhe.Wayethe uyomdayisela zona kanti uzoshaya achithe nazo 
kwamali leyo ayemethembise yona phinde ukuba ayithole. 
Esebanjiwe lapha esiteshini kwaphela konke ukuhlakanipha 
kwasemadolobheni amakhulu nobukwaya bakhe. Ukuveza ukuthi 
ubeyisigebengu ngempela, uzwakala eseyovalelwa emotweni 
yamaphoyisa ethi kuShandu noMkhwanazi, bayohamba besinda, 
ebabiza ngeziphukuphuku. 

Ekugcineni izinkomo zoMkhwanazi noShandu sezisesiteshini, 
esezohamba nazo ngempela umfo kaNdebenkulu, sekuyadaluleka 
ukuthi kanti uyisigebengu esikade sifunwa amaphoyisa esasizibize ngoEE 
Mlomo eMnambithi ngenkathi siqola umfelokazi izinkomo ayezishiyelwe 
umyeni wakhe.Wayethe uyomdayisela zona kanti uzoshaya achithe nazo 
kwamali leyo ayemethembise yona phinde ukuba ayithole. 
Esebanjiwe lapha esiteshini kwaphela konke ukuhlakanipha 
kwasemadolobheni amakhulu nobukwaya bakhe. Ukuveza ukuthi 
ubeyisigebengu ngempela, uzwakala eseyovalelwa emotweni 
yamaphoyisa ethi kuShandu noMkhwanazi, bayohamba besinda, 
ebabiza ngeziphukuphuku. 

Ungomunye wabalingiswa ababalulekile noma engaveli kuzo zonke 
izahluko ezikule noveli. Uvezwe njengomuntu ofuna izinto zihanjiswe 
ngendlela efanele njengoba simthola emhlanganweni owawubizwe 
wuNdebenkulu engumuntu osengathi unekhanda eliqinile. 
NgokukaShandu bekufanele ukuba inkosi yendawo yaseNyanyadu 
uSilosengwe naye ukhona, futhi utsheliwe ngalo mhlangano. Uvezwe 
njengomuntu onakho ukwedelela okunokubhuqa phakathi. Ubiza 
uNdebenkulu ngomfokazi nakuba esezichazile ubukhulu bakhe futhi 
noMgcinisihlalo washo ukuthi uNdebenkulu ngumuntu ohloniphekile 
oze lapha ukuzosiza abantu basemaphandleni abahluphekayo ngoba 
nakhu yena azana futhi ethenjwa abelungu abakhulu. Ubukeka 
engabugqizi qakala lobo bukhulu obufakazelwa nawuMkhwanazi 
ongakaze njalo abezwe nalabo belungu bembiza ngesikwaya. 
Uyaziwa uShandu ukuthi uyayithanda imali. Kuthe uma uNdebenkulu 
eselwenekile udaba lwakhe eze ngalo esebakhombisa nesheke wazisola 
ngamazwi akhe okuvukela uMkhwanazi ngalo Ndebenkulu, kanti 
uza nezindaba ezinhle zokuzobavezela lapho umcebo ulele khona, 


ezinkomeni abazifuyile abalokhu bezidayisela abantu ngemali ephansi 
kakhulu kunale asebeyitshelwa uNdebenkulu. Kuthe noma esehamba 
uNdebenkulu, wazifaka nezakhe izinkomo benoMkhwanazi ukuze 
ziyobalandela umcebo. 
Badumala baphoxeka kakhuku ekugcineni lapho sekuvela ukuthi 
yisigebengu lesi esinguNdebenkulu ebesiqonde ukuzobawaka 
sihambe siyoshona nezinkomo zabo basale bencela izithupha. Wake 
wamthela ngemvubu ephindelela, sekuthi akamudle amfele kwasho 
ukuthi umthetho awumvumeli futhi kuyicala elibi ukushaya umuntu 
sebembophile abomthetho. Nokho zasinda izinkomo zabo babuyela 
nazo emuva.

Into eyivelakancane ? kusuke kushiwo into engajwayelekile, eqabukele 
ibonakele njengoba izimoto ngesikhathi sokubhalwa kwale ndaba 
zaziqabukele zibonakele kuyinto engavamile ukubonakala endaweni 
yaseNyanyadu kwazise nemigwaqo yayingakalungiswa. 

Ukushaya uchithe ? kusho ukuhamba ujubalale ungaphinde ubuye 
njengoba enza umnumzane Mlomo ethathe izinkomo zomfelokazi 
ngoba ethi uyomdayisela zona kubelungu bezindali nabamasilaha. 

Ufokisi ? kushiwo umseshi 

Imbizo ? inhlanganisela yabantu abasuke bebiziwe ukuzohlangana 
ndawonye. Ivame ukubizwa yinkosi ukuzodingida udaba oluthile. 

Isiqhaza ? kushiwo kumuntu onolwazi olungatheni nje, ongafundanga 
kuyaphi.
